PSALM 1 CMEARLPS-M2,1.3

<$$heading>

1.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.5

Blesced be +te man, +tat +gede nou+gt in +te counseil of wicked, ne
stode nou+gt in +te waie of sin+geres, ne sat nau+gt in fals iugement.
CMEARLPS-M2,1.6

2.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.7

Ac hijs wylle was in +te wylle of oure Lord, CMEARLPS-M2,1.8

and he schal +tenche in hijs lawe bo+te daye and ny+gt.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.9

3.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.10

And he schal be as +te tre, +tat hijs sett by +te ernynges of waters;
+tat schal +geue his frut in hijs tyme.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.11

4.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.12

And hijs lef schal nou+gt fallwen; CMEARLPS-M2,1.13

and alle +tynges +tat +te ry+gtful do+t schal multiplien.
CMEARLPS-M2,1.14

5.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.15

Nou+gt so ben +te wicked, nou+gt so; as a poudre, +te wynde caste+t fram
+te face of +ter+te.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.16

6.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.17

For-+ti ne schal nou+gt +te wicked arise in iugement, ne +te sinniers
in +te conseyl of +te ry+gtful.  CMEARLPS-M2,1.18

<P_2>

7.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.20

For oure Lord knew +te waie of +te ry+gtful, CMEARLPS-M2,2.21

and +te waye of synners schal perissen.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.22

PSALM 2 CMEARLPS-M2,2.24

<$$heading>

1.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.26

idel +tynges?  CMEARLPS-M2,2.27

2.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.28

+Te kynges of er+te vpstonden, CMEARLPS-M2,2.29

, CMEARLPS-M2,2.32

4.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.34

5.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.37

+Tan schal God speken to hem in hys wra+te, CMEARLPS-M2,2.38

6.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.40

7.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.42

+Te Lord, oure fader, seide to me, +Tou ert my sone; CMEARLPS-M2,2.43

ich bi+gat +te today wy+t me.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.44

8.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.45

+te terme of +ter+te.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.46

9.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.47

+Tou schalt gouernen hem in sharpnes; CMEARLPS-M2,2.48

10.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.50

& +ge kynges, vnderstonde+t nov; CMEARLPS-M2,2.51

be+t lered, +ge +tat iugen +ter+te.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.52

11.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.53

Serue+t our Lord in doute, CMEARLPS-M2,2.54

and glade+t to hym wy+t quakeing.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.55

12.  CMEARLPS-M2,2.56
